		if (window.recipe_energy && window.recipe_energy.length) {
			let geneated_energy = [];

			for (let i = 0; i < window.recipe_energy.length; i++) {
				let energy = window.recipe_energy[i];
				for (let key in energy) {
					if (energy.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
